*fly¹
/flaɪ ||; flaɪ/verb (present participle flying third person singular present flies;past tense flew /flu: ||; flu/ past participle flown /fləʊn ||; flon/)
1 [I] (used about a bird, insect, aircraft, etc) to move through the air （指鸟类、昆虫、飞机等）飞: This bird has a broken wing and can't fly. 小鸟折了一只翅膀，飞不起来了。 I can hear a plane flying overhead. 我听得见头顶飞过一架飞机。
2 [I,T] to travel or carry sth in an aircraft, etc 坐飞机；空运: My daughter is flying (out) to Singapore next week. 我女儿下星期要坐飞机去新加坡。 Supplies of food were flown (in) to the starving people. 粮食由飞机运给饥民。
3 [I,T] (used about a pilot) to control an aircraft （指飞行员）驾驶（飞机）: You have to have special training to fly a jumbo jet. 必须受过专门训练，才可以驾驶巨型喷气式飞机。
4 [I] to move quickly or suddenly, especially through the air 急速或突然移动（尤指在空中）: A large stone came flying through the window. 打窗口飞进来一块大石头。 I slipped and my shopping went flying everywhere. 我滑了一交，所购之物撒了一地。 Suddenly the door flew open and Mark came running in. 门忽然开了，马克跑进来。 (figurative 比喻) The weekend has just flown by and now it's Monday again. 周末才刚匆匆而过，转眼又到星期一了。
5 [I,T] to move about in the air; to make sth move about in the air 飘扬；使飘扬: The flags are flying. 旗帜迎风飘扬。 to fly a flag/kite 挂旗；放风筝 ☞noun flight 名词为flight
as the crow flies→CROW¹ fly off the handle(informal 非正式) to become very angry in an unreasonable way （莫名其妙地）大发脾气 let fly (at sb/sth)
1 to shout angrily at sb 向…怒吼
2 to hit sb in anger 怒打: She let fly at him with her fists. 她气得打了他几拳。

2 (also flies [pl]) an opening down the front of a pair of trousers that fastens with buttons or another device (a zip)and is covered with a narrow piece of material （裤子的）拉链遮盖，钮扣遮盖 ☞picture on page C6 见C6页插图

flyer
/ˈflaɪə(r) ||; ˈflaɪɚ/ (also flier) noun [C]
1 (informal 非正式) a person who flies a plane (usually a small one, not a passenger plane) 飞行员（通常驾驶非客机的小型飞机）
2 a person who travels in a plane as a passenger （飞机）乘客: frequent flyers 经常乘飞机的人
3 a thing, especially a bird or an insect, that flies in a particular way 飞行物（尤指鸟类或昆虫）: Ducks are strong flyers. 野鸭有很强的飞行能力。
4 a small sheet of paper that advertises a product or an event and is given to a large number of people 广告传单
5 (informal 非正式) a person, an animal or a vehicle that moves very quickly 飞快移动的人、动物或车辆

focus¹
/ˈfəʊkəs ||; ˈfokəs/verb [I,T] (focusing;focused or focussing;focussed)focus (sth) (on sth)
1 to give all your attention to sth 把注意力集中于 [I] to focus on a problem 把注意力集中在一个问题上
2 (used about your eyes or a camera) to change or be changed so that things can be seen clearly （指眼睛或照相机）调节焦距（以看得清楚）: Gradually his eyes focused. 他的眼睛渐渐看清楚了。 I focussed (the camera) on the person in the middle of the group. 我把（照相机）焦点对准站在人群中央的那个人。
focus²
/ˈfəʊkəs ||; ˈfokəs/noun [C] (plural focuses or foci /ˈfəʊsaɪ ||; ˈfosaɪ/)

2 (also focal point) (technical术语) a point at which rays or waves of light, sound, etc meet after REFLECTION or REFRACTION; the point from which rays or waves of light, sound, etc. seem to come （光、声等的）焦点，中心点
in focus/out of focus (used about a photograph or sth in a photograph) clear/not clear （指照片或照片上的东西）清楚或不清楚: This picture is so badly out of focus that I can't recognize anyone. 这张照片照得极不清楚，上面的人我一个也认不出来。

fog
/fɒg; US fɔ:g ||; fɔg/noun [U] [C] thick white cloud that forms close to the land or sea. Fog makes it difficult for us to see 浓雾: Patches of dense fog are making driving dangerous. 浓雾处处，驾驶容易肇祸。 Bad fogs are common in November. 十一月多雾的日子很常见。 Fog is thicker than mist. Haze is caused by heat. Smog is caused by pollution. Look at the note at weather. fog是雾，mist是薄雾或霭。霾(haze)来自热气。烟雾(smog)来自污染。参看weather的注释。

*fold¹
/fəʊld ||; fold/verb

2 [I] fold (up) to be able to be made smaller in order to be carried or stored more easily 可以折迭: This table folds up flat. 这张桌子可以折迭起来。 a folding bed 折迭床
3 [I] fold A in B;fold B round/over A to put sth around sth else 包；裹: I folded the photos in a sheet of paper and put them away. 我用一张纸把照片包好收起来。
4 [I] (used about a business, a play in the theatre, etc) to close because it is a failure （指企业、戏剧等）因失败而结束；倒闭；停演

folk¹
/fəʊk ||; fok/noun
1 (US 美 folks) [pl] (informal 非正式) people in general （泛指）人: Some folk are never satisfied. 有些人永不知足。
2 [pl] a particular type of people 某一类的人: Old folk often don't like change. 老年人往往不爱变化。 country folk 乡下人
3 folks [pl] (informal 非正式) used as a friendly way of addressing more than one person （用于友好地称呼几个人）各位: What shall we do today, folks? 伙计们，我们今天做什么？
4 folks [pl] (informal 非正式) your parents or close relatives 父母；家人；亲戚: How are your folks? 你家里人都好吗？
5 [U] (also folk music) music in the traditional style of a country or community 民间音乐；民谣: Do you like Irish folk? 你喜欢爱尔兰的民间音乐吗？

*follow
/ˈfɒləʊ ||; ˈfɑlo/verb
1 [I,T] to come, go or happen after sb/sth 随后；发生在…之后: You go first and I'll follow (on) later. 你先走，我随后就来。 The dog followed her (around) wherever she went. 她走到哪儿，那条狗就跟到哪儿。 I'll have soup followed by spaghetti. 我想先喝汤，再吃意大利面条。
2 [T] to go along a road, etc; to go in the same direction as sth 沿着某条路等走；向着同一方向走: Follow this road for a mile and then turn right at the pub. 沿着这条路走一英里，到了酒馆再向右拐。 The road follows the river for a few miles. 这条马路沿着河岸延伸几英里。
3 [T] to do sth or to happen according to instructions, an example, what is usual, etc 遵照指示；依据常规: When lighting fireworks, it is important to follow the instructions carefully. 燃放烟火，必须严格遵从指示。 The day's events followed the usual pattern. 这天的活动是按照通常的形式进行的。
4 [I,T] to understand the meaning of sth 领会（意思） · The children couldn't follow the plot of that film. 孩子们看不明白那部电影的剧情。
5 [T] to keep watching or listening to sth as it happens or develops 留心看，倾听，注意（某事物）: The film follows the career of a young dancer. 这部影片描述一位青年舞蹈家的生涯。 Have you been following the tennis championships? 你有没有留意网球锦标赛的消息？
6 [I] follow (on) (from sth) to be the logical result of sth; to be the next logical step after sth 因…而起；是…的必然结果: It doesn't follow that old people can't lead active lives. 不能因此就说，老年人不能过活跃的生活。 Intermediate Book One follows on from Elementary Book Two. 中级第一册紧接初级第二册。
a hard act to follow→HARD¹ as follows used for introducing a list （用于列举事项）如次，如下: The names of the successful candidates are as follows... 及格考生的名单如下… follow in sb's footsteps to do the same job as sb else who did it before you 步某人的后尘；仿效某人: He followed in his father's footsteps and joined the army. 他走他父亲的老路，参了军。 follow sb's example/lead to do what sb else has done or decided to do 仿效某人；按某人的决定做 follow suit to do the same thing that sb else has just done 效法；跟着做 follow your nose to go straight forward 一直往前走: Turn right at the lights and after that just follow your nose until you get to the village. 到了交通灯往右拐，然后一直往前走，直至走到那个村子。 follow sth through to continue doing sth until it is finished 干到底；坚持做完 follow sth up
1 to take further action about sth 对某事采取进一步行动: You should follow up your letter with a phone call. 你应该去信之后再去电话。
2 to find out more about sth 进一步了解；深入调查: We need to follow up the story about the school. 我们须要深入调查关于这所学校的事情。

following¹
/ˈfɒləʊɪŋ ||; ˈfɑloɪŋ/adj
1 next (in time) （时间上）接着的: He became ill on Sunday and died the following day. 他星期天生病，次日就死了。
2 that are going to be mentioned next 下列的: Please could you bring the following items to the meeting... 请带下列东西来开会…
following²
/ˈfɒləʊɪŋ ||; ˈfɑloɪŋ/noun
1 [sing] a group of people who support or admire sth （统称）追随者，支持者: The Brazilian team has a large following all over the world. 巴西队在全世界有一大批支持者。
2 the following [pl] the people or things that are going to be mentioned next 下列的人或事物: The following are the winners of the competition... 以下是比赛优胜者名单…
following³
/ˈfɒləʊɪŋ ||; ˈfɑloɪŋ/prep after; as a result of 之后；由于: Following the riots many students have been arrested. 骚乱过后，很多学生被拘捕。

ˌfollow-ˈthrough
noun [C]
1 (in tennis, golf, etc 网球、高尔夫球等) the final movement you make after you strike the ball ﹙击球后的﹚随球动作，顺势动作
2 the actions that sb takes in order to complete a plan ﹙完成计划所采取的﹚后续行动: We have a great plan, but it can only succeed if the follow-through is good, too. 我们有一个非常好的计划，但要后续行动进展顺利，计划才会成功。

ˈfollow-up
noun [C] something that is done as a second stage to continue or develop sth 后续行动: As a follow-up to the television series, the BBC is publishing a book. 英国广播公司播放完这套电视节目后，将出版一本书。

folly
/ˈfɒli ||; ˈfɑlɪ/noun [C,U] (plural follies) (formal 正式) an act that is not sensible and may have a bad result 愚蠢的行为: It would be folly to ignore their warnings. 谁不理会他们的警告，谁就是傻瓜。

*fond
/fɒnd ||; fɑnd/adj
1 (not before a noun 不用于名词前) fond of sb/sth;fond of doing sth liking a person or thing, or liking doing sth 喜欢某人或某事物；喜欢做某事: Elephants are very fond of bananas. 大象很喜欢吃香蕉。 I'm not very fond of getting up early. 我不大喜欢早起。 Teachers often grow fond of their students. 老师往往会喜欢上他们的学生。
2 (only before a noun 只用于名词前) kind and loving 柔情的；情深的: I have fond memories of my grandmother. 我的祖母给我留下了温馨的回忆。

fondle
/ˈfɒndl ||; ˈfɑndḷ/verb [T] to touch sb/sth gently in a loving or sexual way 爱抚；抚弄

fondly
/ˈfɒndli ||; ˈfɑndlɪ/adv in a loving way 怀着深情；充满感情: Miss Murphy will be fondly remembered by all her former students. 墨菲小姐以前的学生都会满怀深情地怀念她。

fondness
/ˈfɒndnəs ||; ˈfɑndnɪs/noun [U] [sing] (a) fondness (for sb/sth) a liking for sb/sth （对人或事物的）喜爱: I've always had a fondness for cats. 我向来喜欢猫。 My grandmother talks about her schooldays with fondness. 我的祖母满怀深情地谈起她的学生时代。

*fool¹
/fu:l ||; ful/noun [C] a person who is silly or who acts in a silly way 蠢人；傻瓜: I felt such a fool when I realized my mistake. 我发现自己的错误时觉得自己真是一个大傻瓜。 ☞Look at April Fool. 参看April Fool。 make a fool of sb/yourself to make sb/yourself look foolish or silly 使出丑；闹笑话: Barry got drunk and made a complete fool of himself. 巴里喝醉了，出尽洋相。
*fool²
/fu:l ||; ful/verb
1 [T] fool sb (into doing sth) to trick sb 哄骗；欺骗: Don't be fooled into believing everything that the salesman says. 别让推销员把你骗得糊里胡涂的，他说什么你就信什么。
2 [I] to speak without being serious 开玩笑: You didn't really believe me when I said I was going to America, did you? I was only fooling. 你不是真的相信我说的要到美国去吧？我只是开玩笑罢了。
fool about/around to behave in a silly way 做傻事: Stop fooling around with that knife or someone will get hurt! 别再乱耍那把刀子，否则会伤到人。

*foolish

2 looking silly or feeling embarrassed 傻里傻气的；发窘的: I felt a bit foolish when I couldn't remember the man's name. 我想不起那名男子的名字，觉得有点不好意思。 ➔foolishly adv I foolishly agreed to lend him money. 我真傻，竟然答应借给他钱。 ➔foolishness noun [U]

*foot¹
/fʊt ||; fυt/noun (plural feet /fi:t ||; fit/)
1 [C] the lowest part of the body, at the end of the leg, on which a person or animal stands （人或动物的）脚: People usually get to their feet(= stand up) for the national anthem. 奏国歌的时候人们通常站起来。 I usually go to school on foot (= walking). 我通常走路上学。 I need to sit down -- I've been on my feetall day. 我要坐一会儿──我已经站了一整天。 There's broken glass on the floor, so don't walk around in bare feet (= without shoes and socks). 地上有碎玻璃，别光着脚走来走去。 She sat by the fire and the dog sat at her feet. 她坐在炉火旁，小狗坐在她的脚边。 a foot brake/pedal/pump (= one that is operated by your foot) 脚煞车；脚蹬子；脚踏泵 ☞picture at body 见body插图
2 -footed (used to form compound adjectives and adverbs 用于构成复合形容词及副词) having or using the type of foot or number of feet mentioned 有或用那种脚或多少只脚: There are no left-footed players in the team. 队里没有善用左脚的球员。 a four-footed creature 四足动物
3 [C] the part of a sock, etc that covers the foot （袜子等的）脚部
4 [sing] the foot of sth the bottom of sth 底部: There's a note at the foot of the page. 页底有注释。 the foot of the stairs 楼梯底部 the foot of the bed 床尾 [OPP] top 反义词为top
5 [C] (abbr ft) a measurement of length; 30.48 centimetres 英尺（长度单位，相当于30.48厘米）: ‘How tall are you?’ ‘Five foot six (inches).’ “你有多高？”“五英尺六（英寸）。” a six-foot high wall 六英尺高的墙
For more information about measurements look at the special section on numbers at the back of this dictionary. 有关度量衡的详细用法，参看本词典末数词用法部份。 back on your feet completely healthy again after an illness or a time of difficulty （病后）复原；（经历困境后）恢复 be rushed/run off your feet to be extremely busy; to have too many things to do 极其忙碌；疲于奔命: Over Christmas we were rushed off our feet at work. 圣诞节期间，我们工作很忙，简直疲于奔命。 fall/land on your feet to be lucky in finding yourself in a good situation, or in getting out of a difficult situation 运气好；侥幸脱离困境: I really landed on my feet getting such a good job with so little experience. 我经验不足，竟然找到这样一份好工作，真是运气不错。 find your feet→FIND¹ get/have cold feet→COLD¹ get/start off on the right/wrong foot (with sb)(informal 非正式) to start a relationship well/badly 跟某人的关系一开头就不错╱很糟: I seem to have got off on the wrong foot with the new boss. 我跟新老板的关系似乎一开头就很差劲。 have one foot in the grave(informal 非正式) to be so old or ill that you are not likely to live much longer （因年老或疾病）活不长，不久于人世 put your foot down(informal 非正式) to say firmly that sth must (not) happen 坚决反对或阻止: I put my foot down and told Andy he couldn't use our car any more. 我态度坚决，告诉安迪他不能再用我们的车。 put your foot in it(informal 非正式) to say or do sth that makes sb embarrassed or upset 说出冒犯别人或令人发窘的话；做出冒犯别人或令人发窘的事 put your feet up to sit down and relax, especially with your feet off the floor and supported 坐下休息（尤指把双腿搁起来）: I'm so tired that I just want to go home and put my feet up. 我很累，只想回家休息一会儿。 set foot in/on sth→SET¹ stand on your own (two) feet to take care of yourself without help; to be independent 不依靠他人；独立 under your feet in the way; stopping you from working, etc 阻碍着某人: Would somebody get these children out from under my feet and take them to the park? 谁愿意把这些碍手碍脚的孩子领开，带他们上公园去？

*for¹
/fə(r);strong form fɔ:(r) ||; fɚ; fɔr/prep
1 showing the person that will use or have sth （引出使用者或所有者）: Here is a letter for you. 这是你的信。 He made lunch for them. 他给他们做午饭。 It's a book for children. 这是一本儿童读物。
2 in order to do, have or get sth （表示目的）: What's this gadget for? 这玩意儿是做什么用的？ What did you do that for (= Why did you do that)? 你干吗那样做？ Do you learn English for your job or for fun? 你学英语是为了工作还是为了兴趣？ She asked me for help. 她求我帮忙。 Phone now for information. 马上打电话查询一下。 to go for a walk/swim/drink 去散步╱游泳╱喝一杯
3 in order to help sb/sth 为了帮助…: What can I do for you? 你需要些什么？ You should take some medicine for your cold. 你该吃点药治感冒。 Doctors are fighting for his life. 医生们正在抢救他。 shampoo for dry hair 干性头发的洗发剂
4 in support of (sb/sth) 支持: Are you for or against shops opening on Sundays? 商店在星期天开门做生意，你赞成不赞成？
5 meaning sth or representing sb/sth 意为…；代表…: What's the ‘C’ for in ‘BBC’? BBC的C代表什么？ What's the Russian for ‘window’? window在俄语里叫什么？ She plays hockey for England. 她代表英格兰打曲棍球。
6 showing the place that sb/sth will go to （引出目的地）: Is this the train for Glasgow? 这是到格拉斯哥去的火车吗？ They set off for the shops. 他们出发去买东西。
7 (showing a reason) as a result of （引出原因）由于: Ben didn't want to come for some reason. 阿本由于某种原因不想来。 He was sent to prison for robbery. 他因为抢劫而坐牢。 I couldn't speak for laughing. 我笑得连话也说不了。
8 (showing the price or value of sth); in exchange for （引出价钱或价值）以…为代价: I bought this car for £2000. 这辆汽车我花了2000英镑买下来的。 You get one point for each correct answer. 每答对一题得一分。 I want to exchange this sweater for a larger one. 这件套衫我想换一件尺寸大一点的。 The officer was accused of giving secret information for cash. 那名官员被指控为了钱出卖机密情报。
9 showing a length of time （表示一段时间）: I'm going away for a few days. 我要外出几天。 for a while/a long time/ages 经过一会儿╱很长时间╱极长时间 They have left the town for good (= they will not return). 他们已经离开这个镇，永远不回来了。 He was in prison for 20 years (= he is not in prison now). 他坐过20年牢。 He has been in prison for 20 years (= he is still in prison). 他坐牢坐了20年了。
Since is used with a point in time for showing when something began He has been in prison since 1982. Ago is also used for showing when something began He went to prison 20 years ago. since用于指事情从时间上的某一点开始﹕He has been in prison since 1982. 从1982年起，他一直在坐牢。ago也表示某事在什么时候开始﹕He went to prison 20 years ago. 他20年前开始坐牢。
10 showing how many times sth has happened （表示某事发生了多少次）: I'm warning you for the last time. 这是我最后一次警告你。 I met him for the second time yesterday. 昨天我跟他第二次碰头。
11 at a particular, fixed time 在某个特定或固定的时间: What did they give you for your birthday? 你生日的时候他们送给你什么？ Shall we have eggs for breakfast? 我们早餐吃鸡蛋，好不好？ I'm going to my parents' for Christmas. 我要去父母那儿过圣诞节。 The appointment is for 10.30. 约会定在10点半。
12 showing a distance （表示距离）: He walked for ten miles. 他走了十英里路。
13 (after an adjective 用于形容词后) showing how usual, suitable, difficult, etc sb/sth is in relation to sb/sth else （表示相比之下有多平常、合适或困难等）: She's tall for her age. 以她的年龄，她长得算高了。 It's quite warm for January. 就一月份来说，这样的天气算是暖和的了。 It's unusual for Alex to be late. 亚历克斯迟到是不寻常的事。 I think Sandra is perfect for this job. 我认为桑德拉做这工作很合适。
be (in) for it (Brit 英) (informal 非正式) to be going to get into trouble or be punished 惹来麻烦；必受惩罚: If you arrive late again you'll be in for it. 再迟到的话你会受到惩罚的。 for all in spite of 尽管；虽然: For all his money, he's a very lonely man. 他虽然有钱，可是非常寂寞。 for ever→FOREVER(1)
for²
/fə(r);strong form fɔ:(r) ||; fɚ; fɔr/ conj (formal 正式) because 因为；由于: The children soon lost their way, for they had never been in the forest alone before. 那些孩子从没独自到过那森林，所以过不多久就迷路了。

*forbid
/fəˈbɪd ||; fɚˈbɪd/verb [T] (present participle forbidding;past tense forbade or forbad /fəˈbæd ||; fɚˈbæd/ past participle forbidden /fəˈbɪdn ||; fɚˈbɪdṇ/)
1 (usually passive 通常用于被动语态) to not allow sth 不准；不许: Smoking is forbidden inside the building. 大厦内不准吸烟。
2 forbid sb to do sth to order sb not to do sth 不准或禁止某人做某事: My parents forbade me to see Tim again. 父母不让我再跟蒂姆来往。

forbidding
/fəˈbɪdɪŋ ||; fɚˈbɪdɪŋ/adj looking unfriendly or frightening 冷峻的；吓人的: The coast near the village is rather grey and forbidding. 村旁沿海一带气氛萧索，令人望而生畏。

*force¹
/fɔ:s ||; fɔrs/noun
1 [U] physical strength or power 力；力量: The force of the explosion knocked them to the ground. 爆炸的威力把他们震倒在地。 The police used force to break up the demonstration. 警察使用武力驱散了示威群众。
2 [U] power and influence 说服力；影响: the force of public opinion 舆论的威力
3 [C] a person or thing that has power or influence 有影响力的人或物: Britain is no longer a major force in international affairs. 在国际事务中，英国已不再举足轻重了。 Julia has been the driving force behind the company's success. 朱莉娅一直是公司取得成功的推动力。
4 [C] a group of people who are trained for a particular purpose （接受训练执行特定职务的）部队，队伍: a highly trained workforce 训练有素的劳动队伍 the police force 警察部队
5 (usually plural 通常用复数) the soldiers and weapons that an army, etc has 军队等的士兵及武器: the armed forces 武装力量
6 [C,U] (technical术语) a power that can cause change or movement 能够引起改变或移动的力: the force of gravity 万有引力 magnetic/centrifugal force 磁力；离心力 ☞picture at hydraulic 见hydraulic插图
7 [C] [usu.sing] a measure of wind strength 风力等级: a force 9 gale 9级大风
bring sth/come into force to start using a new law, etc; to start being used 实施（新法规等）；开始生效: The government want to bring new anti-pollution legislation into force next year. 政府有意在明年实施新的反污染法规。 force of habit if you do sth from or out of force of habit, you do it in a particular way because you have always done it that way in the past 习惯势力 in force
1 (used about people) in large numbers （指人）大批地: The police were present in force at the football match. 这场足球赛有大批警察在场维持秩序。
2 (used about a law, rule, etc) being used （指法律、规则等）施行中，已生效: The new speed limit is now in force. 新的车速限制已经生效。
join forces (with sb) to work together in order to achieve a shared goal 同…联合或合作（以便实现共同目标）
*force²
/fɔ:s ||; fɔrs/verb[T]
1 force sb (to do sth);force sb (into sth/doing sth) to make sb do sth that he/she does not want to do 强迫: She forced herself to speak to him. 她硬着头皮跟他说话。 The President was forced into resigning. 总统被迫辞职了。
2 to use physical strength to do sth or to move sth 用力干某事或搬动某物: The window had been forced (open). 窗子给撬开了。 We had to force our way through the crowd. 我们不得不从人群里挤出去。
3 to make sth happen when it will not happen naturally 勉强作出: to force a smile/laugh 强作笑颜；勉强哈哈一笑 To force the issue, I gave him until midday to decide. 为了促成那件事，我限他在正午以前作出决定。
force sb's hand to make sb do sth that he/she does not want to do, or make him/her do it sooner than intended 迫使某人做某事或提前做某事

*forget
/fəˈget ||; fɚˈgɛt/verb (past tense forgot /fəˈgɒt ||; fɚˈgɑt/ past participle forgotten /fəˈgɒtn ||; fɚˈgɑtṇ/)
1 [T] forget (doing) sth to not be able to remember sth 忘记: I've forgotten what I was going to say. 我忘了要说的话。 I've forgotten her telephone number. 我忘了她的电话号码。 He forgot that he had invited her to the party. 他忘了自己曾邀请她参加酒会。 I'll never forget meeting my husband for the first time. 我永远也忘不了跟我丈夫初次见面的情景。
2 [I,T] forget (about) sth;forget to do sth to fail to remember to do sth that you ought to have done 忘了做（应做的事） [I] ‘Why didn't you come to the party?’ ‘Oh dear! I completely forgot about it!’ “你怎么没有来参加酒会？”“哎呀！我根本都忘了！” [I] ‘Did you feed the cat?’ ‘Sorry, I forgot.’ “你喂猫了没有？”“对不起，我忘了。” Don't forget to do your homework! 别忘了做功课！
3 [T] to fail to bring sth with you 忘了带（某物）: When my father got to the airport he realized he'd forgotten his passport. 爸爸到了机场才想起忘了带护照。
When we are talking about something we have forgotten, and we want to say where it is, we have to use the word leave. We CANNOT say: ‘He forgot his passport at home’. We have to say: ‘He left his passport at home’. 把东西丢在什么地方要用leave。不可说He forgot his passport at home，应说He left his passport at home。
4 [T] forget (about) sb/sth;forget about doing sth to make an effort to stop thinking about sb/sth; to stop thinking that sth is possible 不再放在心上；忘掉: Forget about your work and enjoy yourself! 别想着工作，好好玩吧！ ‘I'm sorry I shouted at you.’ ‘Forget it. ’ (= don't worry about it) “抱歉我不该对你大叫大嚷。”“别放在心里。”

*forgive
/fəˈgɪv ||; fɚˈgɪv/verb [T] (past tense forgave /fəˈgeɪv ||; fɚˈgev/ past participle forgiven /fəˈgɪvn ||; fɚˈgɪvən/)
1 forgive sb/yourself (for sth/for doing sth) to stop being angry towards sb for sth that he/she has done wrong 原谅；宽恕: I can't forgive his behaviour last night. 我原谅不了他昨晚的所作所为。 I can't forgive him for his behaviour last night. 我原谅不了他昨晚的所作所为。 I can't forgive him for behaving like that last night. 我原谅不了他昨晚的所作所为。
2 forgive me (for doing sth) used for politely saying sorry （客套话，表示请见谅）恕我: Forgive me for asking, but where did you get that dress? 恕我打扰，这件连衣裙你在哪里买的？ ➔forgiveness noun [U]: He begged for forgiveness for what he had done. 他请求原谅他的所作所为。

*fork¹
/fɔ:k ||; fɔrk/noun[C]
1 a small metal object with a handle and two or more points (prongs)that you use for lifting food to your mouth when eating 餐叉；叉子: a knife and fork 一副刀叉
2 a large tool with a handle and three or more points (prongs) that you use for digging the ground 耙: a garden fork 花园里用的耙 ☞picture at garden 见garden插图
3 a place where a road, river, etc divides into two parts; one of these parts （路、河等的）分岔处；岔道；岔流: After about two miles you'll come to a fork in the road. 你走两英里左右，就会到达一个岔口。
*fork²
/fɔ:k ||; fɔrk/verb[I]
1 (used about a road, river, etc) to divide into two parts （指路、河等）分岔: Bear right where the road forks at the top of the hill. 到了山顶的岔口就向右拐。
2 to go along the left or right fork of a road 沿着岔路（向左或右）走: Fork right up the hill. 到了岔口向右拐上山。
fork out (for sth)(informal 非正式) to pay for sth when you do not want to （不愿意地）付钱: I forked out over £20 for that book. 那本书是我花了20多英镑买下来的。

*form¹
/fɔ:m ||; fɔrm/noun
1 [C] a particular type or variety of sth or a way of doing sth 形式；方式: Swimming is an excellent form of exercise. 游泳是一种很好的运动。 We never eat meat in any form. 我们从来什么荤也不吃。
2 [C,U] the shape of sb/sth 形状；形体: The articles will be published in book form. 这些文章将汇编成书出版。
3 [C] an official document with questions on it and spaces where you give answers and personal information 表格: an entry form for a competition 参赛表格 to fill in an application form 填写申请表
4 [C] a class in a school 年级
In Britain, the years at secondary school used to be called first/second/third, etc form but now they are called Year 7 to Year 11. However the last two years of school (for pupils aged between 16 and 18) are still referred to as the sixth form. 在英国，中学的一、二、三…年级过去叫做first／second／third…form，如今叫做Year 7…Year 11。然而，最后两学年（16岁到18岁之间的学生就读）仍然叫做六年级(the sixth form)。
5 [C] (grammar语法) a way of spelling or changing a word in a sentence （词语、拼写等的）形式: the irregular forms of the verbs 动词的不规则形式 The plural form of mouse is mice. mouse的复数形式是mice。
6 [U] the state of being fit and strong for a sports player, team, etc （运动员、运动队等的）竞技状态: to be in/out of form 竞技状态甚佳╱欠佳
7 [U] how well sb/sth is performing at a particular time, for example in sport or business （在特定时候的）表现（如运动或企业的）: to be on/off form 表现甚佳╱欠佳 On present form the Italian team should win easily. 按照目前的表现，意大利队应当很容易取胜。
true to form→TRUE
*form²
/fɔ:m ||; fɔrm/verb
1 [I,T] to begin to exist or to make sth exist （使）开始存在: A pattern was beginning to form in the monthly sales figures. 每月的销售额开始形成一种模式。 These tracks were formed by rabbits. 这些足迹是兔子留下的。
2 [T] to make or organize sth 形成；组成: to form a government 筹组政府 In English we usually form the past tense by adding ‘-ed’. 英语的过去时一般以加上-ed的形式出现。
3 [T] to become or make a particular shape 成为或构成某种形状: The police formed a circle around the house. 警察围圈包围了这座房子。 to form a line/queue 排成一行╱一队
4 linking verb to be the thing mentioned 是…的组成部份；构成: Seminars form the main part of the course. 研讨会是这个课程的主要部份。 The survey formed part of a larger programme of market research. 这次调查是市场研究这个更大项目的一环。
5 [T] to begin to have or think sth 开始有或考虑（某事）: I haven't formed an opinion about the new boss yet. 我对这位新上司还没有什么看法。 to form a friendship 发展成友谊

*formal
/ˈfɔ:ml ||; ˈfɔrmḷ/adj
1 (used about language or behaviour) used when you want to appear serious or official and in situations in which you do not know the other people very well （指言语或行为）正式的，庄重的，拘谨的: ‘Yours faithfully’ is a formal way of ending a letter. Yours faithfully是正式信函的一种结语。 She has a very formal manner -- she doesn't seem to be able to relax. 她这个人非常拘谨，看来不懂得放松自己。 a formal occasion (= one where you must behave politely and wear the clothes that people think are suitable) 正式场合
In this dictionary some words and phrases are marked (formal) or (informal). This will help you to choose the right word for a particular situation. Often there is an informal or neutral word with a similar meaning to a more formal one. 为了帮助读者选用得体的词语，本词典在某些词语旁边标上了“正式”(formal)或“非正式”(informal)字样。正式场合适用的词语，一般有相应的非正式场合适用的词语或中性词。
2 official 正式的；正规的: I shall make a formal complaint to the hospital about the way I was treated. 我要就我所受到的待遇向医院正式提出申诉。 [OPP] informal 反义词为informal ➔formally /-məli ||; -mḷɪ/ adv

formaldehyde
/fɔ:ˈmældɪhaɪd ||; fɔrˈmældəˌhaɪd/noun [U]:
1 (symbol CH₂O) a colourless gas with a strong smell 甲醛（无色气体，有浓烈气味）
2 (also formalin /ˈfɔ:məlɪn ||; ˈfɔrməlɪn/) a liquid made by mixing formaldehyde and water, used especially for keeping examples of animals, plants, etc (specimens)in a good condition for a long time so that they can be studied by experts or scientists 甲醛溶液（由甲醛和水混合而成，用于保存动植物标本）

formality
/fɔ:ˈmæləti ||; fɔrˈmælətɪ/noun (plural formalities)
1 [C] an action that is necessary according to custom or law 手续；仪式: There are certain formalities to attend to before we can give you a visa. 你办好一些手续以后，我们便可以把签证发给你。
If an action is just a formality, we mean that people think that it is necessary according to custom or law but that it has no real importance or effect otherwise. just a formality表示只根据习惯或法律上的规定办事，并无实质意义或效用。
2 [U] careful attention to rules of language and behaviour 遵守语言或行为规范

format¹
/ˈfɔ:mæt ||; ˈfɔrmæt/noun [C] the shape of sth or the way it is arranged or produced 版式；版面；编排: It's the same book but in a different format. 这是同一本书，但版式不同。
format²
/ˈfɔ:mæt ||; ˈfɔrmæt/verb [T] (formatting;formatted)
1 (computing计算机技术) to prepare a computer disk so that data can be recorded on it 为计算机磁盘编排格式；格式化: to format a disk 把磁盘格式化
2 to arrange text on a page or a screen 在纸上或屏幕上编排文本；使（文本）格式化: to format a letter 编排一封信

formation
/fɔ:ˈmeɪʃn ||; fɔrˈmeʃən/noun
1 [U] the act of making or developing sth 形成；组成: the formation of a new government 新政府的筹组
2 [C,U] a number of people or things in a particular shape or pattern 队形；组成方式: rock formations 岩层 A number of planes flew over in formation. 几架飞机编队从上空掠过。 formation dancing 团体舞

formative
/ˈfɔ:mətɪv ||; ˈfɔrmətɪv/adj having an important and lasting influence (on sb's character and opinions) （对性格或见解）影响深远的: A child's early years are thought to be the most formative ones. 儿童幼年时期据认为对性格发展最具影响力。

*former
/ˈfɔ:mə(r) ||; ˈfɔrmɚ/adj (only before a noun 只用于名词前) of an earlier time; belonging to the past 前些时候的；以前的: Ronald Reagan, the former American President 前任美国总统罗讷德˙里根 In former times people often had larger families. 以往的家庭往往比现在的大。

*formerly
/ˈfɔ:məli ||; ˈfɔrmḷɪ/adv in the past; before now 过去；以前: the country of Myanmar (formerly Burma) 缅甸（Myanmar，以前叫Burma） The hotel was formerly a castle. 这家酒店的前身是个城堡。 Used to be is a more common way of saying was formerly The hotel used to be a castle. used to be可表示was formerly的意思，且较常用：The hotel used to be a castle.这家酒店原本是个城堡。
formidable
/ˈfɔ:mɪdəbl ||; ˈfɔrmɪdəbḷ/adj
1 causing you to be quite frightened 相当可怕的: His mother is a rather formidable lady. 他母亲令人望而生畏。
2 difficult to deal with; needing a lot of effort 难对付的；艰巨的；繁重的: Reforming the education system will be a formidable task. 改革教育制度将是一件艰巨的任务。

formula
/ˈfɔ:mjələ ||; ˈfɔrmjələ/noun [C] (plural formulas or formulae /-li: ||; -ˌli/)
1 (technical术语) a group of signs, letters or numbers used in science or mathematics to express a general law or fact 分子式；公式；方程式: What is the formula for converting miles to kilometres? 用什么公式把英里换算做公里？
2 a list of (often chemical) substances used for making sth; the instructions for making sth 配方；处方: The formula for the new vaccine has not yet been made public. 新疫苗的配方仍未公诸于世。
3 a formula for (doing) sth a plan of how to get or do sth 计划；方案: What is her formula for success? 她成功的诀窍是什么？ Unfortunately, there's no magic formula for a perfect marriage. 很遗憾，世上没有能使婚姻十全十美的灵丹妙方。

formulate
/ˈfɔ:mjəleɪt ||; ˈfɔrmjəˌlet/verb[T]
1 to prepare and organize a plan or ideas for doing sth 制订（计划）；构想（意念）: to formulate a plan 制订计划
2 to express sth (clearly and exactly) （清楚而确切地）阐述，表达: She struggled to formulate a simple answer to his question. 她力求简单明了地回答他的问题。

forsake
/fəˈseɪk ||; fɚˈsek/verb [T] (past tense forsook /fəˈsʊk ||; fɚˈsυk/ past participle forsaken /fəˈseɪkən ||; fɚˈsekən/) (old-fashioned 旧) to leave a person or a place for ever (especially when you should stay) 永远离开（地方），抛弃（人）（尤指不应当地）

forthcoming
/ˌfɔ:θˈkʌmɪŋ ||; ˈfɔrθˈkʌmɪŋ/adj
1 that will happen or appear in the near future 即将发生或出现的: Look in the local paper for a list of forthcoming events. 想知道有什么活动快要举行，看看当地的报纸吧。
2 (not before a noun 不用于名词前) offered or given 接获；获得: If no money is forthcoming, we shall not be able to continue the project. 如果没有现成的资金，这个项目我们就不能继续下去。
3 (not before a noun 不用于名词前) (used about a person) ready to be helpful, give information, etc （指人）乐于提供协助、信息等: Kate isn't very forthcoming about her previous job, so I don't know what she did exactly. 凯特不大愿意谈她以前的工作，因此我不知道她究竟是做什么的。

*fortune
/ˈfɔ:tʃu:n ||; ˈfɔrtʃən/noun
1 [C,U] a very large amount of money 一大笔钱: I always spend a fortune on presents at Christmas. 我每年都花一大笔钱买圣诞礼物。 She went to Hollywood in search of fame and fortune. 她到好莱坞去追逐名利。
2 [U] chance or the power that affects what happens in a person's life; luck 运气: Fortune was not on our side that day (= we were unlucky). 我们那天真倒霉。 [SYN] fate 同义词为fate
3 [C] [usu.pl] the things (both good and bad) that happen to a person, family, country, etc （个人、家庭、国家等的）命运，运气: The country's fortunes depend on its industry being successful. 这个国家的命运有赖于工业兴盛。
4 [C] what is going to happen to a person in the future 一个人的将来；命运: Show me your hand and I'll try to tell your fortune. 把你的手给我看看，我来给你算算命。 [SYN] fate or destiny 同义词为fate或destiny

*forward¹
/ˈfɔ:wəd ||; ˈfɔrwɚd/adv
1 (also forwards) in the direction that is in front of you; towards the front, end or future 向前；朝着前方、终点或未来: Keep going forward and try not to look back. 一直向前走，不要回头看。 [OPP] back or backward(s) 反义词为back或backward(s)
2 in the direction of progress; ahead 进展中；前进: The new form of treatment is a big step forward in the fight against Aids. 这种新疗法把与艾滋病的斗争推进了一大步。
Forward is used after many verbs, for example bring, come, look, put. For the meaning of the expressions look at the verb entries. 很多动词的后面都用得着forward，如bring、come、look、put。关于这些词语的意义，可参看有关动词的词条。 backward(s) and forward(s)→BACKWARDS put the clock/clocks forward/back→CLOCK¹
*forward²
/ˈfɔ:wəd ||; ˈfɔrwɚd/adj
1 (only before a noun 只用于名词前) towards the front or future 向前的；为将来的: forward planning 有关未来的计划

3 behaving towards sb in a way that is too confident or too informal 放肆的；冒失的: I hope you don't think I'm being too forward, asking you so many questions. 我问了你那么多问题，但愿你不会觉得我太没有礼貌。

2 to help to improve sth or to make sth progress 促进；助长: I'm trying to forward my career in publishing. 我正努力促进自己的出版事业。

foster
/ˈfɒstə(r); US ˈfɔ:- ||; ˈfɔstɚ/verb[T]
1 (especially Brit 尤为英) to take a child who needs a home into your family and to care for him/her without becoming the legal parent 寄养育，寄抚养（抚养别人的孩子，但不作为法律上的父母）: to foster a homeless child 抚育一个无家可归的孩子
The people who do this are foster-parents. The child is a foster-child. Look at adopt. 寄养父母叫做foster-parents，寄养子女叫做foster-child。参看adopt。

/faʊl ||; faυl/adj
1 that smells or tastes disgusting （气味或味道）令人恶心的: a foul-smelling cigar 极难闻的雪茄烟 This coffee tastes foul! 这咖啡味道差极了！
2 (especially Brit 尤为英) very bad or unpleasant 很糟的；坏的: Careful what you say -- he's in a foul temper/mood. 说话可要小心，他心情很不好。 The foul weather prevented our plane from taking off. 天气恶劣，我们的飞机不能起飞。
3 (used about language) very rude; full of swearing （指言语）粗鄙的，猥亵的: foul language 脏话
fall foul of sb/sth to get in trouble with sb/sth because you have done sth wrong 触犯: At sixteen she fell foul of the law for the first time. 她首次犯法是在十六岁的时候。
foul²
/faʊl ||; faυl/verb
1 [I,T] (used in sports) to attack another player in a way that is not allowed （指体育）以不允许的方式攻击对手，犯规: Shearer was fouled inside the box and the referee awarded his team a penalty. 希勒在罚球区内遭对方犯规，裁判判给他的队一个点球。
2 [T] to make sth dirty (with rubbish, waste, etc) （以垃圾等）弄脏: Dogs must not foul the pavement. 狗不得弄脏人行道。
foul sth up(spoken 口语) to spoil sth 把…搞糟: The delay on the train fouled up my plans for the evening. 火车误点，把我晚上的计划全打乱了。

/ˈfrækʃn ||; ˈfrækʃən/noun[C]
1 a small part or amount 小部份；少量；一点儿: For a fraction of a second I thought the car was going to crash. 我有一剎那以为要撞车了。
2 a division of a number 分数: 1/2 and 1/4 are fractions. 1/2和1/4都是分数。 ☞Look at vulgar fraction and integer. 参看vulgar fraction及integer。

fractional distillation
/ˌfrækʃənl dɪstɪˈleɪʃn ||; ˌfrækʃənḷ dɪstɪlˈeʃən/noun [U] (technical术语) the process of separating the parts of a liquid mixture by heating it. As the temperature goes up, each part in turn becomes a gas, which then cools as it moves up a tube and can be collected as a liquid. 分馏

fractionally
/ˈfrækʃənəli ||; ˈfrækʃənḷɪ/adv to a very small degree; slightly 轻微地；稍稍: fractionally faster/taller/heavier 略快╱高╱重

fracture
/ˈfræktʃə(r) ||; ˈfræktʃɚ/noun [C,U] a break in a bone or other hard material 骨折；断裂；破裂 fracture verb [I,T] She fell and fractured her ankle. 她栽了一交，把脚腕子摔断了。 A water pipe fractured and flooded the bathroom. 有根水管裂了，弄得浴室里满地是水。

fragile
/ˈfrædʒaɪl; US -dʒl ||; ˈfrædʒəl/adj easily damaged or broken 易损坏的；易碎的: This bowl is very fragile. Please handle it carefully. 这只碗很脆，小心点儿拿。

fragment¹
/ˈfrægmənt ||; ˈfrægmənt/noun [C] a small piece that has broken off or that comes from sth larger 碎片: The builders found fragments of Roman pottery on the site. 建筑工人在工地捡到了一些古罗马陶器的碎片。 I heard only a fragment of their conversation. 他们的对话，我只听了个片言只语。
fragment²
/frægˈment ||; frægˈmɛnt/verb [I,T] (formal 正式) to break (sth) into small pieces 使破碎；打碎: The country is becoming increasingly fragmented by civil war. 国家因内战而日趋分裂。

fragrance
/ˈfreɪgrəns ||; ˈfregrəns/noun [C,U] a pleasant smell 芬香；芬芳

/ˈfreɪgrənt ||; ˈfregrənt/adj having a pleasant smell 芬香的；芬芳的

frail
/freɪl ||; frel/adj weak or not healthy 虚弱的；不健康的: My aunt is still very frail after her accident. 姑母遇意外后，到现在仍然十分虚弱。

/ˈfreɪlti ||; ˈfreltɪ/noun [C,U] (plural frailties) weakness of a person's body or character （身体或性格上）软弱，脆弱，虚弱

*frame¹
/freɪm ||; frem/noun[C]
1 a border of wood or metal that goes around the outside of a door, picture, window, etc （门、画、窗等的）框: a window frame 窗框
2 the basic strong structure of a piece of furniture, building, vehicle, etc which gives it its shape （家具、建筑物、车辆等的）骨架，支架: the frame of a bicycle/an aircraft 自行车╱飞机的骨架 ☞picture at bicycle 见bicycle插图
3 [usu.pl] a structure made of plastic or metal that holds the two pieces of glass (lenses) in a pair of glasses 眼镜框 ☞picture at glasses 见glasses插图
4 [usu.sing] the basic shape of a human or animal body （人或动物的）体格，骨架: He has a large frame but he's not fat. 他个子大，可不算胖。
frame of mind a particular state or condition of your feelings; the mood 心情；心境；情绪: I'm not in the right frame of mind for a party. I'd prefer to be on my own. 我心情不好，不想去酒会，宁可一个人清静点。
frame²
/freɪm ||; frem/verb[T]
1 to put a border around sth (especially a picture or photograph) （给图画、照片等）装框: Let's have this photograph framed. 我们给这张相片配个框吧。
2 (usually passive 通常用于被动语态) to give false evidence against sb in order to make him/her seem guilty of a crime 罗织罪名；提供伪证；诬陷: The man claimed that he had been framed by the police. 这个男人说他被警方诬陷了。
3 (formal 正式) to express sth in a particular way 以某种方式表达: The question was very carefully framed. 这个问题问得很谨慎。

framework
/ˈfreɪmwɜ:k ||; ˈfremˌwɝk/noun[C]
1 the basic structure of sth that gives it shape and strength 骨架；结构: A greenhouse is made of glass panels fixed in a metal framework. 温室以金属为骨架，架上镶着一大块一大块的玻璃板。 (figurative 比喻) the basic framework of society 社会的基本结构
2 a system of rules or ideas which help you decide what to do 方案；蓝图: The plan may be changed but it will provide a framework on which we can build. 这个方案也许会变，但我们可以此为基本构想。

franc

franchise
/ˈfræntʃaɪz ||; ˈfræntʃaɪz/noun

2 [U] (formal 正式) the right to vote in elections 选举权；投票权

frank
/fræŋk ||; fræŋk/adj showing your thoughts and feelings clearly; saying what you mean 坦诚的；坦率的: To be perfectly frank with you, I don't think you'll pass your driving test. 老实告诉你，我想这次驾驶考试你通不过。 ➔frankly adv Please tell me frankly what you think about my idea. 你对我的想法有什么意见，不妨跟我直说。 ➔frankness noun [U]

frantic
/ˈfræntɪk ||; ˈfræntɪk/adj
1 extremely worried or frightened 极度忧虑的或恐慌的；狂乱的: The mother went frantic when she couldn't find her child. 那母亲找不到孩子，急得像发了疯似的。 frantic cries for help 焦灼的呼救声
2 very busy or done in a hurry 忙乱的；忙的: a frantic search for the keys 慌忙找钥匙 We're not busy at work now, but things get frantic at Christmas. 我们眼下工作不忙，但到了圣诞节会忙得不得了。 ➔frantically /-kli ||; -kḷɪ/ adv

fraud

fraught
/frɔ:t ||; frɔt/adj
1 fraught with sth filled with sth unpleasant 充满（令人不快的事物）: a situation fraught with danger/difficulty 危机四伏╱困难重重的局面
2 (used about people) worried and nervous; (used about a situation) very busy so that people become nervous （指人）忧心忡忡的；（指情况）忙乱得叫人紧张的: Things are usually fraught at work on Mondays. 每逢星期一，工作通常忙乱不堪。

fray
/freɪ ||; fre/verb[I,T]
1 if cloth, etc frays or becomes frayed, some of the threads at the end start to come apart （布等的末端）磨散，磨损: This shirt is beginning to fray at the cuffs. 这件衬衣的袖口快要磨破了。 [T] a frayed rope 磨损的绳子
2 if a person's nerves, etc fray or become frayed, he/she starts to get annoyed 使烦躁；使（神经）紧张: Tempers began to fray towards the end of the match. 比赛快要结束的时候，人们的心情开始紧张起来。

/fri:k ||; frik/noun[C]

2 a very unusual and strange event, person, animal, etc 怪异的事、人、动物等；不寻常的（事、人、动物等）: a freak accident/storm/result 反常的事故╱风暴╱结果 The other kids think Ally's a freak because she doesn't watch TV. 阿利不看电视，别的孩子认为她是个怪人。

*free¹
/fri: ||; fri/adj
1 not in prison, in a cage, etc; not held or controlled 自由的: The government set Mandela freein 1989. 政府于1989年释放了曼德拉。 There is nowhere around here where dogs can run free. 在这一带，哪里也不准狗随便乱跑。
2 free (to do sth) not controlled by the government, rules, etc 不受（政府、规则等）操纵的，控制的；自由的: There is free movement of people across the border. 人们可以自由进出边境。 free speech/press 言论╱新闻自由
3 costing nothing 免费的: Admission to the museum is free/free of charge. 博物馆免费入场。 Children under five usually travel free on trains. 五岁以下的儿童乘火车通常免费。
4 not busy or being used 有空的；未被占用的: I'm afraid Mr Spencer is not free this afternoon. 斯潘塞先生恐怕今天下午没有空。 I don't get much free time. 我没有很多闲工夫。 Is this seat free? 这个座位有人了吗？
5 free from/of sth not having sth dangerous, unpleasant, etc 没有危险的；没有不快的: free of worries/responsibility 没有烦恼╱责任 free from pain 没有痛楚
feel free→FEEL¹ free and easy informal or relaxed 不拘礼节；轻松: The atmosphere in our office is very free and easy. 我们办公室气氛十分轻松自在。 get, have, etc a free hand to get, have, etc permission to make your own decisions about sth 有自主权 of your own free will because you want to, not because sb forces you 出于自愿
*free²
/fri: ||; fri/verb[T]
1 free sb/sth (from sth) to let sb/sth leave or escape from a place where he/she/it is held 释放: to free a prisoner 释放囚犯 The protesters freed the animals from their cages. 示威群众把笼里的动物放了出来。
2 free sb/sth of/from sth to take away sth that is unpleasant from sb 使脱离令人不快的事物: The medicine freed her from pain for a few hours. 这药解除她的痛楚达几个小时。
3 free sb/sth (up) for sth;free sb/sth (up) to do sth to make sth available so that it can be used; to put sb in a position in which he/she can do sth 使某物能供使用；使某人能干某事: If I cancel my trip, that will free me to see you on Friday. 如果我取消旅行，我就有时间在星期五来看望你。

*freeze¹
/fri:z ||; friz/verb (past tense froze /frəʊz ||; froz/ past participle frozen /ˈfrəʊzn ||; ˈfrozṇ/)
1 [I,T] to become hard (and often change into ice) because of extreme cold; to make sth do this 结冰；冷藏；冷冻: Water freezes at 0° Celsius. 水在零摄氏度结冰。 The ground was frozen solid for most of the winter. 冬天的大部份时间里，地面都冻得硬邦邦的。 [T] frozen peas/fish/food 冷冻豌豆╱鱼类╱食品
2 [I] used with ‘it’ to describe extremely cold weather when water turns into ice （跟it一起用，指天气）冷得使水结冰，严寒: I think it's going to freeze tonight. 我看今晚准冷得要命。
3 [I,T] to be very cold or to die from cold 寒冷；冻死: It was so cold on the mountain that we thought we would freeze to death. 山上那么冷，我们以为会冻死的。 Turn the heater up a bit -- I'm frozen stiff. 暖炉开大点儿，我给冻僵了。
4 [I] to stop moving suddenly and completely because you are frightened or in danger （因惊吓或危险而）突然停止移动；吓呆: The terrible scream made her freeze with terror. 那凄厉的叫声把她吓呆了。 Suddenly the man pulled out a gun and shouted ‘Freeze!’ 那个男子突然掏出枪，大喝一声﹕“别动！”
5 [T] to keep the money you earn, prices, etc at a fixed level for a certain period of time. 冻结（工资、物价等）: Spending on defence has been frozen for one year. 国防开支已经冻结一年。

/ˈfrenzi ||; ˈfrɛnzɪ/noun [sing] [U] a state of great emotion or activity that is not under control 狂躁；狂乱: There's no need to get in a frenzy -- you've got until Friday to finish your essay. 你们没有必要慌里慌张，文章星期五才要求完成。 I could hear a frenzy of activity in the kitchen. 我听见厨房里一阵躁动。

frequency
/ˈfri:kwənsi ||; ˈfrikwənsɪ/noun (plural frequencies)
1 [U] the number of times sth happens in a particular period 频率（在特定时间内某种事情发生的次数）: Fatal accidents have decreased in frequency in recent years. 近几年死亡事故发生的频率已经下降。
2 [U] the fact that sth happens often 频繁: The frequency of child deaths from cancer near the nuclear power station is being investigated. 在核电厂附近地区，经常有儿童死于癌症，有关当局对这个现象正在进行调查。
3 [C,U] the rate at which a sound wave or radio wave moves up and down (vibrates) 频率（声波或无线电波振动的次数）: high-frequency/low-frequency sounds 高╱低频声 ☞picture at wavelength 见wavelength插图

*fresh
/freʃ ||; frɛʃ/adj
1 (used especially about food) produced or picked very recently; not frozen or in a tin （尤指食品）刚生产的，刚采摘的，新鲜的: fresh bread/fruit/flowers 新鲜面包；新鲜水果；鲜花 ☞Look at stale. 参看stale。
2 left somewhere or experienced recently 新近留在某处的；刚经历过的；新的: fresh blood/footprints 鲜血；新的脚印 Write a few notes while the lecture is still fresh in your mind. 趁着对那一课还记忆犹新，赶快做些笔记吧。
3 new and different 新而不同的: They have decided to make a fresh start in a different town. 他们已决定在另一个市镇重头干起。 I'm sure he'll have some fresh ideas on the subject. 我敢说，在这个问题上他准有一些新的想法。
4 (used about water) without salt; not sea water （指水）淡水的
5 pleasantly clean or bright 清新的；鲜明的: Open the window and let some fresh air in. 打开窗子放点新鲜空气进来。
6 not tired 不疲倦的；精神的: I'll think about the problem again in the morning when I'm fresh. 明天早上我精神好的时候再想想这问题吧。
7 fresh from/out of sth having just finished sth 刚刚做完（某事）: Life isn't easy for a young teacher fresh from university. 对于刚刚踏出大学校门的年轻教师来说，日子并不轻松。 ➔freshly adv freshly baked bread 刚出炉的面包 ➔freshness noun [U]

/ˈfrendli ||; ˈfrɛndlɪ/adj (friendlier;friendliest)

5 in which the people, teams, etc taking part are not competing seriously 和睦共处的；不激烈竞争的: a friendly argument 友好的争论 I've organized a friendly match against my brother's team. 我组织了一场对我弟弟所属球队的友谊赛。 ➔friendliness noun [U]

*from
/frəm;strong form frɒm ||; frəm; frɑm/prep
1 showing the place, direction or time that sb/sth starts or started （表示开始的地方、方向或时间）: She comes home from work at 7 o'clock. 下班后，她通常7点钟回到家里。 a cold wind from the east 寒冷的东风 Water was dripping from the tap. 水龙头在滴水。 Peter's on holiday from next Friday. 下个星期五彼得开始度假了。 The supermarket is open from 8a.m. till8p.m. every day. 这家超级市场每天上午8点开门，晚上8点关门。
2 showing the person who sent or gave sth （表示送、给等动作的施发人）: I borrowed this jacket from my sister. 这件夹克是我跟妹妹借来的。 a phone call from my father 我爸爸打来的电话
3 showing the origin of sb/sth （表示来源）: ‘Where do you come from?’ ‘I'm from Australia.’ “你是哪里人？”“我是澳大利亚人。” cheeses from France and Italy 法国和意大利出产的奶酪 quotations from Shakespeare 莎翁名句
4 showing the material which is used to make sth （指出原料）: Paper is made from wood. 纸是用木料制成的。 This sauce is made from cream and wine. 这种调料是用奶油和葡萄酒配制的。
Made of tells us the material the object actually consists of a table made of wood a house made of bricks made of表示物品实际上由哪种材料构成﹕a table made of wood木头桌子·a house made of bricks砖头房子
5 showing the distance between two places （表示两地的距离）: The house is five miles from the town centre. 这幢房子离镇中心有五英里路。 I work not far from here. 我的工作单位离这儿不远。
6 showing the point at which a series of prices, figures, etc, start （表示价格、数字等幅度的下限）: Our prices start from £2.50 a bottle. 我们的售价从2.5英镑一瓶起。 Tickets cost from £3 to £11. 票价从3英镑到11英镑不等。
7 showing the state of sb/sth before a change （表示改动之前的状态）: The time of the meeting has been changed from 7 to8 o'clock. 会议时间已经由7点钟改为8点钟。 The article was translated from Russian intoEnglish. 这篇文章是由俄语译成英语。 Things have gone from bad to worse. 情况每况愈下。
8 showing that sb/sth is taken away, removed or separated from sb/sth else （表示被带走、移走或分开）: Children don't like being separated from their parents for a long period. 孩子不喜欢跟父母分开太久。 (in mathematics) 8 from 12 leaves 4. （数学）12减8剩4。
9 showing sth that you want to avoid （表示要避免或防止的事物）: There was no shelter from the wind. 没有避风的地方。 This game will stop you from getting bored. 这游戏会叫你不再觉得无聊。
10 showing the cause of sth （表示原因）: People in the camps are suffering from hunger and cold. 营里的人又饿又冷。
11 showing the reason for making a judgement or forming an opinion （表示作出判断或形成看法的原因）: You can tell quite a lot from a person's handwriting. 你可以从一个人的笔法了解很多东西。
12 showing the difference between two people, places or things （表示人、地或事物的不同）: Can you tell margarine from butter? 你能分辨出人造黄油和黄油吗？ Is Portuguese very different from Spanish? 葡萄牙语是不是跟西班牙语很不相同？
from… on starting at a particular time and continuing for ever 从某时间起一直: She never spoke to him again from that day on. 打那天起，她没有再跟他说过半句话。 From now on you must earn your own living. 以后你要自食其力了。

frond
/frɒnd ||; frɑnd/noun[C]
1 a long leaf, often divided into parts along the edge, of some plants or trees （棕榈类等的）长叶: the fronds of a palm tree 棕榈树叶子
2 a long piece of SEAWEED (= a plant that grows in the sea) that looks like one of these leaves （藻类的）藻体

*front¹
/frʌnt ||; frʌnt/noun
1 the front [C] [usu.sing] the side or surface of sth/sb that faces forward 正面；前面: a dress with buttons down the front 正面直行扣钮的连衣裙 the front of a building (= the front wall) 建筑物的正面 a card with flowers on the front 正面有花的图案的贺卡 She slipped on the stairs and spilt coffee all down her front. 她在楼梯上滑了一交，衣服前面泼满了咖啡。
2 the front [C] [usu.sing] the most forward part of sth; the area that is just outside of or before sb/sth （某人或某物）前面: Young children should not travel in the front of the car. 小孩坐汽车不该坐前座。 There is a small garden at the front of the house. 屋前有个小花园。
On the front of means ‘on the front surface of sth ’ The number is shown on the front of the bus. In front (of sth) means ‘further forward than another person or thing ’; before sb/sth else A car has stopped in front of the bus. There were three people in front of me in the queue. At/In the front (of sth) means ‘in the most forward part inside sth ’ The driver sits at the front of the bus. Look at these sentences too The teacher usually stands in front of the class. The noisy children were asked to sit at the front of the class (= in the front seats). on the front指“在…的正面”：The number is shown on the front of the bus.公共汽车的路线号码标在正面。in front (of sth)指“在前方”：A car has stopped in front of the bus.公共汽车的前边停了一辆汽车。·There were three people in front of me in the queue.我前面还排了三个人。at／in front of (sth)指“在前部”：The driver sits at the front of the bus.公共汽车司机坐在车子最前端的地方。再看以下句子：The teacher usually stands in front of the class.老师通常站在全班学生面前。·The noisy children were asked to sit at the front of the class. (=in the front seats)吵闹的孩子被分配坐在前排座位。
3 [C] a particular area of activity 领域: Things are difficult on the domestic/political/economic frontat the moment. 眼下国内╱政治╱经济方面有困难。 Progress has been made on all fronts. 各方面都取得了进展。
4 the front [sing] the line or area where fighting takes place in a war 前线；战线: to be sent to the front 被派到前线
5 [sing] a way of behaving that hides your true feelings 表面的行为或样子: His brave words were just a front. He was really feeling very nervous. 他的豪言壮语只为掩饰，其实他心里很紧张。
6 [C] a line or area where warm air and cold air meet 锋，锋面（冷暖气团交汇的地带）: A cold front is moving in from the north. 冷锋正从北面移入。 ☞picture at cloud 见cloud插图
back to front→BACK¹ in front further forward than sb/sth; ahead 领先于；在…前面: Some of the children ran on in front. 有一些孩子跑在前面。 After three laps the Kenyan runner was in front. 跑了三圈后，肯尼亚选手领先。 in front of sb/sth
1 in a position further forward than but close to sb/sth 在…之前不远处: The bus stops right in front of our house. 这路公共汽车在我家的门前有个站。 Don't stand in front of the television. 别站在电视机前面。 The book was open in front of her on the desk. 她面前桌上摊着一本书。 In front of does not mean the same as opposite. in front of和opposite意思不同。 ☞picture at opposite 见opposite插图
2 if you do sth in front of sb, you do it when that person is there in the same room or place as you 在…的面前（做某事）: I couldn't talk about that in front of my parents. 我在爸妈面前不能谈那件事。
up front(informal 非正式) as payment before sth is done 预先支付: I want half the money up front and half when the job is finished. 我想先支一半工资，做完了再支另一半。
front²
/frʌnt ||; frʌnt/adj (only before a noun 只用于名词前) of or at the front (1,2) 正面的；前部的；前面的: the front door/garden/room 正门；前花园；起居室 sit in the front row 坐在前排 front teeth 门牙

/ˈfrʌntɪə(r); US frʌnˈtɪər ||; frʌnˈtɪr/noun

*frost¹
/frɒst; US frɔ:st ||; frɔst/noun [C,U] the weather condition when the temperature falls below 0° Celsius (freezing point) and a thin layer of ice forms on the ground and other surfaces, especially at night 严寒，霜冻（冰点以下结霜的天气状况）: There was a hard frost last night. 昨晚有严重霜冻。 It will be a chilly night with some ground frost. 今晚将很寒冷，地面会有霜冻。

/frɒst; US frɔ:st ||; frɔst/verb [T] (especially US 尤为美) =ICE² frost over/up to become covered with a thin layer of ice 盖满了霜: The window has frosted over/up. 窗上披着一层白霜。 ☞Look at defrost. 参看defrost。

/fʊlˈfɪl ||; fυlˈfɪl/ (US 美 fulfill) verb [T] (fulfilling;fulfilled)

*full¹
/fʊl ||; fυl/adj
1 holding or containing as much or as many as possible 充满的；满的: The bin needs emptying. It's full up (= completely full). 垃圾箱满了，要把它倒干净。 a full bottle 盛得满满的瓶子 The bus was full so we had to wait for the next one. 那班公交车挤满了人，我们只好等下一班。 (figurative 比喻) We need a good night's sleep because we've got a full (= busy) day tomorrow. 我们要好好睡一觉，明天忙着呢。
2 full of sb/sth containing a lot of sb/sth 有很多人或物: The room was full of people. 房间里挤满了人。 His work was full of mistakes. 他干的活儿错漏百出。 The children are full of energy. 孩子们精力充沛。
3 full (up) having had enough to eat and drink 饱的；吃喝够了的: No more, thank you. I'm full (up). 不要啦，谢谢你，我吃饱了。
4 (only before a noun 只用于名词前) complete; not leaving anything out 完整的；没有遗漏的: I should like a full report on the accident, please. 关于这次事故，请给我一份详尽的报告。 Full details of today's TV programmes are on page 20. 今天的电视节目详情刊在第20页。 He took full responsibility for what had happened. 对于所发生的事，他愿意负全部责任。 Please give your full name and address. 请写上你的全名和详细地址。
5 (only before a noun 只用于名词前) the highest or greatest possible 最高的；最大的: She got full marks in her French exam. 她的法语考了满分。 The train was travelling at full speed. 火车正全速行驶。
6 full of sb/sth/yourself thinking or talking a lot about sb/sth/yourself 想个没完；说个没完: When she got back from holiday she was full of everything they had seen. 她度假回来后，满口所见所闻，说个没完。 He's full of himself (= thinks that he is very important) since he got that new job. 他自从担任新职务后就自高自大起来。
7 round in shape 丰满的；圆鼓鼓的: She's got quite a full figure. 她体态很丰满。 He's quite full in the face. 他有一张大圆脸。
8 (used about clothes) made with plenty of material （指衣服）宽松的: a full skirt 宽裙子
at full stretch working as hard as possible 拚命，全力（工作）: When the factory is operating at full stretch, it employs 800 people. 那家工厂全面开工的时候，雇员达800人。 full of beans/life with a lot of energy and enthusiasm 充满活力和热情: They came back from holiday full of beans. 他们度假归来，精神焕发。 have your hands full→HAND¹ in full with nothing missing; completely 全部: Your money will be refunded in full (= you will get all your money back). 全部款项都会退回给你。 Please write your name in full. 请你写上全名。 in full swing at the stage when there is the most activity 正全力进行中；正处于活跃阶段: When we arrived the party was already in full swing. 我们抵达酒会的时候，气氛已经十分热烈。 in full view (of sb/sth) in a place where you can easily be seen 在容易被看见的地方: In full view of the guards, he tried to escape over the prison wall. 他在警恒的视线中企图越过监狱的围墙逃跑。 to the full as much as possible 充分: to enjoy life to the full 尽情享受生活

*fun¹
/fʌn ||; fʌn/noun [U] pleasure and enjoyment; an activity or a person that gives you pleasure and enjoyment 乐趣；带来乐趣的人或活动: We had a lot of funat the party last night. 昨晚的舞会我们玩得很开心。 The party was great fun. 这舞会挺有意思的。 Have fun (= enjoy yourself)! 尽情玩吧！ It's no fun having to get up at 4 o'clock every day. 每天得4点钟起床可不是好玩的。 (just) for fun/for the fun of it (just) for amusement or pleasure; not seriously （只是）为乐趣；非认真地: I don't need English for my work. I'm just learning it for fun. 我的工作用不着英语，我学英语只是为了乐趣。 in fun as a joke 说着玩儿: It was said in fun. They didn't mean to upset you. 他们说着玩儿，并不想惹你不快。 make fun of sb/sth to laugh at sb/sth in an unkind way; to make other people do this 取笑；使取笑: The older children are always making fun of him because of his accent. 年纪大的小孩常爱拿他的口音来开玩笑。 poke fun at sb/sth→POKE
*fun²
/fʌn ||; fʌn/adj amusing or enjoyable 有趣的；令人愉快的: to have a fun time/day out 玩得很快活；在外面快活地玩一天 Brett's a fun guy. 布雷特是个很有意思的人。 Be careful. Funny describes something or someone that makes you laugh or that is strange. It is not the same as fun Jane is fun (= I enjoy being with her). Jane is funny (= she tells jokes and makes me laugh all the time/she is strange). 注意：funny形容事物或人滑稽、古怪，含义与fun不同：Jane is fun. 简是个很有意思的人（我很喜欢跟她作伴）。·Jane is funny.简是个很滑稽的人（她老说笑话，逗得我笑个不停╱她是个怪人）。
*function¹
/ˈfʌŋkʃn ||; ˈfʌŋkʃən/noun[C]
1 the purpose or special duty of a person or thing 职能；功能: The function of the heart is to pump blood through the body. 心脏的功能是把血液压送到全身。 to perform/fulfil a function 履行╱完成职能
2 an important social event, ceremony, etc 社交盛会；仪式: The princess attends hundreds of official functions every year. 公主每年出席数以百计的官方活动。
3 (mathematics数学) a quantity whose value depends on the varying values of others. In the statement 2x=y, y is a function of x. 函数（其值取决于其他变量的值。在2x=y中，y是x的函数）
function²
/ˈfʌŋkʃn ||; ˈfʌŋkʃən/verb [I] to work correctly; to be in action 发挥作用；运转: Only one engine was still functioning. 只有一部发动机仍在运转。 [SYN] operate 同义词为operate

functional
/ˈfʌŋkʃənl ||; ˈfʌŋkʃənḷ/adj
1 practical and useful rather than attractive 有实际用途的: cheap functional furniture 又便宜又实用的家具
2 working; being used 运作中；发挥功能: The system is now fully functional. 这个制度已经在全面实行。

functionality
/ˌfʌŋkʃəˈnæləti ||; ˌfʌŋkʃəˈnælətɪ/noun [C,U] (plural functionalities) (computing计算机技术) the set of functions that a computer or other electronic system can perform （计算机或其他电子系统的）一套功能: new software with additional functionality 有附加功能的新软件

ˈfunction key
noun [C] (computing计算机技术) one of the KEYS on a computer which are used to perform a particular operation （计算机的）功能键

*fund¹
/fʌnd ||; fʌnd/noun
1 [C] a sum of money that is collected for a particular purpose 专款；基金: They contributed £30 to the disaster relief fund. 他们捐了30英镑给救灾基金。
2 funds [pl] money that is available and can be spent 资金: The hospital is trying to raise funds for a new kidney machine. 医院正筹集资金买一台新的血液透析器。
fund²
/fʌnd ||; fʌnd/verb [T] to provide a project, school, charity etc with money 提供资金；资助；拨款: The Channel Tunnel is not funded by government money. 海峡隧道并非由政府拨款兴建。

fundamental
/ˌfʌndəˈmentl ||; ˌfʌndəˈmɛntḷ/adj basic and important; from which everything else develops 基本的；重要的；根本的: There will be fundamental changes in the way the school is run. 该校的运作方式将有重大变革。 There is a fundamental difference between your opinion and mine. 你我的意见有重大的分歧。 ➔fundamentally /-təli ||; -tḷɪ/ adv The government's policy has changed fundamentally. 政府政策已有根本的改变。

fundamentals
/ˌfʌndəˈmentlz ||; ˌfʌndəˈmɛntḷz/noun [pl] basic facts or principles 基本事实或原则

ˈfund-raiser
noun [C] a person whose job is to find ways of collecting money for a charity or an organization 资金筹集者；募捐者 ➔fund-raising noun [U]: fund-raising events 募捐活动

*funeral
/ˈfju:nərəl ||; ˈfjunərəl/noun [C] a ceremony (usually religious) for burying or burning a dead person 葬礼（通常指宗教性质的）: The funeral will be held next week. 葬礼将在下周举行。 The body of the dead person is carried in a coffin, on which there are often wreaths of flowers. The coffin is buried in a grave or is burned (cremated). 葬礼中死者躺在棺木(coffin)里，棺木上面常常放了花圈(wreath)。棺木或埋在坟墓(grave)里，或进行火化(cremate)。

=UNDERTAKER

ˈfuneral parlour

/ˈfʌnfeə(r) ||; ˈfʌnˌfɛr/ =FAIR²(1)

fungicide
/ˈfʌŋgɪsaɪd ||; ˈfʌndʒəˌsaɪd/noun [C,U] a substance that kills a type of plant with no leaves or flowers(fungus)that grows on other plants or animals and harms them 杀真菌剂；杀菌剂

fungus
/ˈfʌŋgəs ||; ˈfʌŋgəs/noun [C,U] (plural fungi /-gaɪ ||; -gaɪ/or funguses) a plant that is not green and does not have leaves or flowers (for example a MUSHROOM ), or that is like a wet powder and grows on old wood or food, walls, etc. Some fungi can be harmful. 真菌 ☞Look at mould and toadstool. 参看mould及toadstool。 ➔fungal adj a fungal disease/infection/growth 真菌疾病╱感染╱肿瘤

funk
/fʌŋk ||; fʌŋk/noun [U] a type of modern dance music with a strong rhythm 乡土爵士乐﹙节奏强劲﹚

funky
/fʌŋki ||; ˈfʌŋkɪ/adj (funkier; funkiest) (informal 非正式)
1 (used about music) having a strong rhythm that is easy to dance to ﹙音乐﹚节奏强适宜跳舞的: a funky disco beat 适宜跳舞的迪斯科强节
2 fashionable and unusual, in a good way 时髦独特的: She wears really funky clothes. 她穿的衣服真是时髦又独特。
3 having an unusual and unpleasant smell 有恶臭的；有怪味的: This milk smells funky—do you think it's okay to drink it? 这牛奶闻起来有怪味——你认为可以喝吗？

funnel
/ˈfʌnl ||; ˈfʌnḷ/noun[C]
1 an object that is wide at the top and narrow at the bottom, used for pouring liquid, powder, etc into a small opening 漏斗 ☞pictures at kitchen and laboratory 见kitchen及laboratory插图
2 the metal chimney of a ship, engine, etc （轮船、蒸汽机车的）金属烟囱

funnily
/ˈfʌnɪli;-əli ||; ˈfʌnɪlɪ; -əlɪ/adv in a strange or unusual way 奇怪；古怪: She's walking very funnily. 她走路的样子很古怪。 funnily enough used for expressing surprise at sth strange that has happened （表示对某事感到吃惊、意外）说也奇怪，真奇怪: Funnily enough, my parents weren't at all cross about it. 奇怪的是，我父母对这件事一点也不生气。

*funny
/ˈfʌni ||; ˈfʌnɪ/adj (funnier;funniest)
1 that makes you smile or laugh 滑稽的；好笑的: a funny story 一个滑稽的故事 He's an extremely funny person. 他这个人非常滑稽。 That's the funniest thing I've heard in ages! 那是我好久以来听到过的最滑稽的事！
2 strange or unusual; difficult to explain or understand 怪异的；难以解释的；难以理解的: Oh dear, the engine is making a funny noise. 咦，发动机的声音好怪呀。 It's funny that they didn't phone to let us know they couldn't come. 他们来不了也不给我们挂个电话，真奇怪。 That's funny -- he was here a moment ago and now he's gone. 真奇怪，他方才明明在这儿，现在却不见了。 Can I sit down for a minute? I feel a bit funny(= a bit ill). 我有点不舒服，可以坐一会儿吗？ ☞Look at the note at fun ². 参看fun^2的注释。

ˈfunny bone
noun [C] [usu.sing] (informal 非正式) the bone at your elbow, containing a very sensitive nerve that is painful if you hit it against sth （肘部的）鹰嘴突；肱骨内髁

*fur
/fɜ:(r) ||; fɝ/noun

furious
/ˈfjʊəriəs ||; ˈfjυrɪəs/adj
1 furious (with sb);furious (at sth) very angry 勃然大怒的；大发雷霆的: He was furious with her for losing the car keys. 她把汽车钥匙丢了，他气得暴跳如雷。 He was furious at having to catch the train home. 他得赶火车回家，心里真光火。 ☞noun fury 名词为fury
2 very strong; violent 强烈的；猛烈的: A furious row has broken out over the closure of the school. 就是否关闭学校的问题爆发了激烈的争论。 ➔furiously adv

furnish
/ˈfɜ:nɪʃ ||; ˈfɝnɪʃ/verb [T] to put furniture in a room, house, etc （在房间、房子等里面）放置家具: The room was comfortably furnished. 这房间里有舒适的家具。 ➔furnished adj She's renting a furnished room in Birmingham. 她将在伯明翰租个带家具的房间。

*furniture
/ˈfɜ:nɪtʃə(r) ||; ˈfɝnɪtʃɚ/noun [U] the things that can be moved, for example tables, chairs, beds, etc in a room, house or office 家具: modern/antique/second-hand furniture 现代╱古董╱二手家具 garden/office furniture 花园／办公室家具 Be careful. ‘Furniture’ is an uncountable noun They only got married recently and they haven't got much furniture. If we are talking about an individual item we must say ‘a piece of furniture ’ The only nice piece of furniture in the room was an antique desk. 注意：furniture是不可数名词：They only got married recently and they haven't got much furniture.他们结婚不久，家里没有什么家具。一件家具叫做a piece of furniture: The only nice piece of furniture in the room was an antique desk. 房间里象样的家具就只有一张古董书桌。

furrow
/ˈfʌrəʊ ||; ˈfʌro/noun[C]
1 a line in a field that is made for planting seeds in by a farming machine that turns the earth (plough) （田里的）犁沟
2 a deep line in the skin on a person's face, especially on the forehead （脸上的）皱纹（尤指前额上的） ☞Look at wrinkle. 参看wrinkle。

furry

*further¹
/ˈfɜ:ðə(r) ||; ˈfɝðɚ/adj adv
1 more; to a greater degree 更多；进一步: Are there any further questions ? 还有别的问题吗？ Please let us know if you require any further information. 如需要更多数据，请告诉我们。 I have nothing further to say on the subject. 这个问题我没有别的好说了。 The museum is closed until further notice (= until another announcement is made). 博物馆暂时关闭，重开日期容后公布。 Can I have time to consider the matter further? 能不能给我一点时间把这件事进一步考虑一下？
2 (also farther) (the comparative of far far的比较级) at or to a greater distance in time or space （时间或空间上）更远: It's not safe to go any further. 再往前走不安全。 I can't remember any further back than 1970. 1970年以前的事我已经记不起了。
Further and farther can both be used when you are talking about distance Bristol is further/farther from London than Oxford is. I jumped further/farther than you did. In other senses only further can be used We need a further week to finish the job. 表示距离，further和farther都可以用﹕Bristol is furtherarther from London than Oxford is.布里斯托尔去伦敦要比牛津去伦敦远一点。· I jumped further／farther than you did. 我跳得比你远。表达其他含义则只能用further﹕We need a further week to finish the job.我们还要一个星期才能完成这项工作。 further afield→FAR²
further²
/ˈfɜ:ðə(r) ||; ˈfɝðɚ/verb [T] (formal 正式) to help sth to develop or be successful 促进；推动: to further the cause of peace 促进和平事业

ˌfurther eduˈcation
noun [U] (abbr FE) (Brit 英) education for people who have left school (but not at a university) （为已经离开学校的人开办的）继续教育，进修（但不是大学） ☞Look at higher education. 参看higher education。

fury
/ˈfjʊəri ||; ˈfjυrɪ/noun [U] very great anger 震怒；狂怒: She was speechless with fury. 她气得说不出话来。 ☞adjective furious 形容词为furious

fuse¹
/fju:z ||; fjuz/noun[C]
1 a small piece of wire in an electrical system, machine, etc that melts and breaks if there is too much power. This stops the flow of electricity and prevents fire or damage 保险丝；熔线: A fuse has blown -- that's why the house is in darkness. 保险丝烧断了──所以屋里一片漆黑。 That plug needs a 15 amp fuse. 那个插头需要一根15安培的保险丝。 ☞picture at plug 见plug插图
2 a piece of rope, string, etc or a device that is used to make a bomb, etc explode at a particular time （炸弹的）导火索，引信，信管
fuse²
/fju:z ||; fjuz/verb[I,T]
1 (used about two things) to join together to become one; to make two things do this （指两件事物）融合；使合而为一: As they heal, the bones will fuse together. 两根骨头慢慢愈合，会连在一起。 The two companies have been fused into one large organization. 两家公司已合并成为一家大企业。
2 to stop working because a fuse¹(1) has melted; to make a piece of electrical equipment do this （电器）因保险丝熔断而失灵；使保险丝熔断: The lights have fused. 电灯灭了，是保险丝烧断了。 I've fused the lights. 我让电灯的保险丝给烧断了。

fuselage
/ˈfju:zəlɑ:ʒ ||; ˈfjuzḷˌɑʒ/noun [C] the main part of a plane (not the engines, wings or tail) （飞机的）机身（不包括发动机、机翼、机尾） ☞picture at plane 见plane插图

fusion
/ˈfju:ʒn ||; ˈfjuʒən/noun
1 [U] [sing] the process or the result of joining different things together to form one （不同事物的）融合: the fusion of two political systems 两种不同政治制度的融合
2 (also ˌnuclear ˈfusion) [U] (in physics 物理学) the action or process of combining the central parts(nuclei)of atoms to form a heavier central part(nucleus), with energy being created 核聚变，核融合（原子核聚变成一种更重的核，同时释放能量） ☞Compare fission. 与fission比较。

fuss¹
/fʌs ||; fʌs/noun [sing] [U] a time when people behave in an excited, a nervous or an angry way, especially about sth unimportant （尤指为小事）激动，紧张，气恼；大惊小怪: The waiter didn't make a fuss when I spilt my drink. 我把饮料泼了，服务员没有生气。 What's all the fuss about? 干吗那样大惊小怪？ make/kick up a fuss (about/over sth) to complain strongly 强烈抱怨；大吵大闹 make a fuss of/over sb/sth to pay a lot of attention to sb/sth 过分关怀；过分体贴；娇养: My grandmother used to make a big fuss of me when she visited. 祖母以前一来就对我关怀备至。
fuss²
/fʌs ||; fʌs/verb[I]
1 to be worried or excited about small things 大惊小怪；小题大作: Stop fussing. We're not going to be late. 不要大惊小怪，我们不会迟到的。
2 fuss (over sb/sth) to pay too much attention to sb/sth 过分关心: Stop fussing over all the details. 不要老是纠缠细节。
not be fussed (about sb/sth) (Brit 英) (spoken 口语) to not care very much 不很在乎；不大在意: ‘Where do you want to go for lunch?’ ‘I'm not fussed.’ “你想到哪儿吃午饭？”“随便。”

fussy
/ˈfʌsi ||; ˈfʌsɪ/adj
1 fussy (about sth) (used about people) giving too much attention to small details and therefore difficult to please （指人）爱挑剔的: He is very fussy about food (= there are many things which he does not eat). 他这个人对饮食过分讲究。 ☞Look at particular and picky. 参看particular及picky。
2 having too much detail or decoration 烦琐的；过分修饰的: I don't like that pattern. It's too fussy. 我不喜欢那个图案，太花哨了。

futile
/ˈfju:taɪl; US -tl ||; ˈfjutḷ/adj (used about an action) having no success; useless （指行动）徒劳无功的，无用的: They made a last futile attempt to make him change his mind. 他们最后一次试图让他回心转意，但徒劳无功。 ➔futility noun [U]

futon
/fu:tɒn ||; ˈfutɑn/noun [C] a piece of furniture with a wooden frame and a thin cushion that can be folded and used to sit on, or opened and used as a bed 日本床垫

*future
/ˈfju:tʃə(r) ||; ˈfjutʃɚ/noun
1 the future [sing] the time that will come after the present 未来: Who knows what will happen in the future ? 将来的事谁知道？ in the near/distant future (= soon/not soon) 不远／遥远的将来
2 [C] what will happen to sb/sth in the time after the present 前途: Our children's futures depend on a good education. 孩子的前途是好是坏，要看他们有没有受过良好的教育。 The company's future does not look very hopeful. 公司的前景看来不太乐观。
3 [U] the possibility of being successful 成功的可能性: I could see no future in this country so I left to work abroad. 我觉得留在国内没有前途，所以到国外去工作了。
4 the future (tense) [sing] (grammar语法) the tense of a verb that expresses what will happen after the present 将来时；未来式
For more information about the future tense, look at the Quick Grammar Reference section at the back of this dictionary. 有关将来时的详细用法，参看本词典末“语法便览”部份。 future adj (only before a noun 只用于名词前) She met her future husband when she was still at school. 早在求学时期她就认识了她后来的丈夫。 You can keep that book for future reference (= to look at again later). 那本书你留着用吧，将来可以参考。 in future from now on 以后；今后: Please try to be more careful in future. 以后可要小心点儿。

futuristic
/ˌfju:tʃəˈrɪstɪk ||; ˌfjutʃəˈrɪstɪk/adj
1 extremely modern and unusual in appearance, as if belonging to a future time 极其现代的；未来派的: futuristic design/furniture 极其新潮的设计/家具
2 imagining what the future will be like 幻想未来的: a futuristic novel/movie 幻想未来的小说/电影

fuzzy
/ˈfʌzi ||; ˈfʌzɪ/adj not clear 不清楚的；模糊的: The photo was a bit fuzzy but I could just make out my mother on it. 这张照片有点模糊，我好不容易才认出妈妈来。

FYI
/ˌef waɪ ˈaɪ ||; ˌɛf ˌwaɪ ˈaɪ/abbr (written 书面语) used in writing to mean ‘eor your information’ 供参考

fête
/feɪt ||; fet/noun [C] an outdoor event with competitions, entertainment and things to buy, often organized to make money for a particular purpose （户外举行的）游乐义卖会，园游会: the school/village/church fête 学校╱村╱教会义卖会
